< review>
Rose Hills Rec Center has a great park director Leticia (Letty) she and her assistants are very helpful. There are lots of children activities and a senior group that meets there with many outings. The playground/park area is small, it feels just right for it's size. There is soccer, baseball, basketball, BBQ area with tables and for the toddlers there is a sand box. The playground has gentle rolling hills to sit, relax and take in the beautiful view of the San Gabriel mountains (clear day). On windy days you can fly a kite, and see the white clouds passing in the blue sky. Bring a volleyball net, set it up in the outfield and have a ball. The playground/park is clean and maintain nicely, very nice. May you have fun and enjoy...<//review>

< text>
Rose Hill Recreation playground/park is just the right size, not so big that you lose sight of your children. You can watch your kids play baseball, basketball, or for toddlers they have a secure sand box area. This rec center has soft rolling hills, that you can lay down relax and still have a view of the playground. You can also BBQ under beautiful shaded trees near restrooms and Rec office. So bring the family and friends and enjoy the day. Yes it's a small rec center, but (less is more). Meet and greet, get to know your Rose Hill Rec Center, and your Rose Hills community...</text>

<username>La Morena Fea<//username>< Review>
I am a frequent Carter's customer & have been going to this specific location for quite some time now. I'm always greeted upon entering the store & the employees are always nice & welcoming. During tonight's visit, I was very impressed/satisfied with the service that I received from Ignacio (I hope I spelled his name right). I mentioned using my coupon & he searched high & low to find me one that wasn't expired to add to my purchase (it took him a few minutes). He could have easily given up & said that he couldn't find one like most people would have, but he continued to look until he found one. Now that's GREAT customer service! This location is clean, well stocked, the clothes are suuuuuuuper cute, AND the service is great. It doesn't get any better than that. I will continue to come to this location.<//Review>

< text>
I'll start this by saying everyone in this office was very nice and it was overall a pleasant experience. I'll also say this is my first experience with fillers, so I'm not really an authority on this, I'll just give you the details and let you make your own decisions, and I may update this review in the future if I learn more. I went in for one syringe of lip filler and overall am happy with the results, but I do have that feeling they could be better. This practice uses Restylane only, no Juvederm, and on me they used Restylane Defyne. At my two week check in, I saw there was a bit of asymmetry in my top lip. One side is clearly smaller than the other, and the pink part of the lip is noticeably thinner, especially near the corner. I'm sure it's not VERY noticeable, but I'll let you decide if it would bother you. Also, you can see in the pictures it's bumpy on the larger side. There are quite a few lumps in my lips, but the only one that bothers me really is one on the larger side of my top lip where I can tell the bump is shallow, as if it happened as the needle was being pulled out or something. It is visible all the time, even when I smile. The nurse said she couldn't really see what I was talking about on either concern. She did offer to inject some dissolver into the lump, but I opted to just wait for it to get naturally smaller rather than dissolve some of the filler I paid so much for. Neither thing is really THAT noticeable, but it feels like for 500$ they should not happen, although since this was my first time I really have no idea. Even with those issues, I really do love the results and would probably still recommend, however I will probably be trying somewhere new to compare when this filler wears off.

Update: I was called by the office about this review and while I appreciate the follow up, I want to leave this information here for anyone researching different places to get lip filler. She explained to me they cannot save any filler for adjustments as it is illegal and if they were to make adjustments they would open a new syringe, but I didn뗪 want to spend anymore money on this at this time. They do offer half syringes which are 300$<//text>

My new Samsung Note 20 Ultra has been displaying a "moisture detected" message for a week despite there being no contact with water. I called several places including UBREAKIFIX in Culver City. Out of any of the places I called , Bobby the technician I spoke to, was by far and away the most knowledgeable about what would be needed to attempt repairs . Not only that, but he was incredibly nice and helpful letting me know what parts would be needed and offering to call me when they were available. He actually called Samsung while I was on the phone with him to make sure they would have the right parts since this is a brand new model. When I brought the phone in they were just as nice and helpful in the store as over the phone. They replaced the needed components and the error went away but unfortunately returned during their post fix diagnostics. However Bobby didn't just hand me the phone back and say "sorry we couldn't fix it", he called other stores as well as Samsung again to find out if there might be other options to fix it. Sadly it wasn't something they could fix in the store but I was given detailed information of what to tell Samsung since the phone will have to be repaired by them. Bobby went above and beyond what was needed, and it genuinely seemed like that is his everyday level of service. I was so impressed that when I went back in to pick up the phone I gave him a $20 tip - which he actually refused and said he was just doing his job!!! I would definitely recommend this location, and Bobby in particular, to anyone who needed to have a phone serviced. It's a typical middle of nowhere convenience store. < Text>
I'm more speaking on the side of a Trucker, so that's how I'm rating this (sorry guys who drive cars!), There's a rest stop across the way for us truck drivers, but kept getting reviews on this place when i looked at the rest stop.  If your driving and need space, this Chevron has more parking then most truck stops. People say that the supplies and food is overpriced, but honestly i didn't see much of a difference between this place and other stops ive been too. They also have some neat gifts and collectables near the front. Lady who ran the register was very nice and friendly. They'll have most things that you need for food and basic supplies here. Only thing that isn't great is that they aren't open 24 -7, so can't get anything in the middle of the night. There are a few port o-lets out in the front if you need to use the bathroom and store is closed.<//Text>
